{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"Scandinavian Pendant Lights Full of Warmth From Secto Design","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445633","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/scandinavian-pendant-lights-full-of-warmth-from-secto-design/victo-4250-victo-small-4251-3/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Secto-Design-Victo-Small-Featured-Image-810x582.jpg\" alt=\"Scandinavian Pendant Lights Full of Warmth From Secto Design\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Known for lighting that features innovative, architectural forms, <a href=\"https://www.sectodesign.fi/en-us\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Secto Design</a> has welcomed two new pendant lights to their family. With a wooden warmth that suits a variety of styles, <a href=\"https://www.sectodesign.fi/en-us/pendant/victo-small-4251-pendant-lamp#pendant\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Victo Small 4251</a> and <a href=\"https://www.sectodesign.fi/en-us/pendant/owalo-7000-pendant#pendant\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Owalo 7000</a> join the brand&#8217;s 26 <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/lighting\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">lighting</a> options.</p>\n<p>Looking for an inviting illumination that&#8217;s welcoming and cozy? Victo knows how to gather people around a table. A smaller version of the original larger Victo, this pendant is a wonderful solution for tighter spaces that&#8217;s both visually light yet captivating. Group together several – or mix with another collection – to make an even bigger impact.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445646\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445646\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445646\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Secto-Design-Victo-Small-Living-7-810x609.jpg\" alt=\"living space\" width=\"810\" height=\"609\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Secto-Design-Victo-Small-Living-7-810x609.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Secto-Design-Victo-Small-Living-7-800x601.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Secto-Design-Victo-Small-Living-7-768x577.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Secto-Design-Victo-Small-Living-7.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>But if am impact is what you&#8217;re after, and you have the space, you may want to explore the Owalo. At three feet wide it gives dining spaces and meeting rooms alike a pleasant atmosphere. The focal point of whatever room it inhabits, Owalo also features a diffuser and dimmer.</p>\n<p>All of Secto&#8217;s lighting products are designed by Finnish architect Seppo Koho, and handmade by craftspeople in Finland using local, top quality PEFC-certified Finnish birchwood. Their lights are available in natural birch, laminated in white or black or in walnut veneer.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445644\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445644\" cf705fd8891c.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617817081498},{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 Substance","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445778","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/beast-health-b10-blends-style-with-substance/beast-health-00016/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00016-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"The Beast Health B10 Blends Style With Substance\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/beast-health\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Beast Health</a> arrives as the new kid on the block of appliance startups, but the company&#8217;s founder Colin Sapire can claim knowing more than a thing or two about the personal blender category. In fact he helped create it. His previous efforts are responsible for bringing the world the NutriBullet, <em>the</em> appliance most synonymous with the health meals on-the-go lifestyle. Sapire returns with another personal health appliance, this one noticeably upgraded in both form and function: the <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/beast-health/products/b10-health-blender\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Beast Health B10 Health Blender</a>.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445882\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445882\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445882\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0001-810x900.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"900\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0001-810x900.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0001-800x889.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0001-768x853.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0001.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Noting Millennials and Gen Z have proven to be health conscious generations, the B10 Health Blender arrives swathed in industrial design and branding clearly communicating its intended to appeal to a demographic used to good design as the rule rather than an exception (we&#8217;re especially partial to the Pebble Grey version with its mango orange push button).</p>\n<p><iframe src=\"https://player.vimeo.com/video/523015303?color=e8e8e8&#38;title=0&#38;byline=0&#38;portrait=0\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p>\n<p><a style=\"letter-spacing: 0.13px;\" href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445877\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445877\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445877\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00020-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00020-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00020-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00020-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00020.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/beast-health/products/b10-health-blender\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">B10 Health Blender&#8217;s</a> lantern-like design is constructed from extruded, forged and CNC machined aluminum, finished with protective matte powder coated finish; that solid finish and the weight that comes with it imparts the B10 with a premium feel that definitely stands out from its cheaper infomercial competitors. There&#8217;s also heft (12lbs) to provide enough downward stabilization while its 1000-watt motor works its magic in either pulse or blend mode, blades capable of spinning at 18,000 rpm for cavitation to transform ingredients from solids into a liquid state (if you want to know more about what exactly happens within a blender, <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iCmjZboscPM\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">this video</a> illustrates the process in dramatic slo-motion).</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445878\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445878\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445878\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-HOME-BANNER-02-810x405.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"405\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-HOME-BANNER-02-810x405.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-HOME-BANNER-02-800x400.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-HOME-BANNER-02-768x384.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-HOME-BANNER-02.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The B10&#8217;s most distinguishing design detail – a 12-Rib vessel – may seem purely aesthetic at first glance. But Beast Health notes the shape was an engineered decision, one chosen to optimize the amount of internal turbulence created within the B10 while in blend or pulse mode, resulting in improved blending efficiency compared to a smooth surface interior.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445879\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445879\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445879\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-445879 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0006-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0006-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0006-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0006-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-0006.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The B10&#8217;s double thick vessel paired with a leak-resistant cap design resulted in a seal that securely kept powdered smoothies + hemp milk concoctions, homemade salad dressings and hummus safely contained and easy to pour or spoon out. While there&#8217;s only two modes, the B10 is pre-programmed with a minute-long blending cycle that simplified morning smoothies into a 1-button affair.</p></div>\n<div id=\"attachment_445880\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445880\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445880\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-445880 https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-2-000011-SQUARE-02-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-2-000011-SQUARE-02.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">All Beast Health vessels are BPA and BPS-free for those concerned with chemical leaching into their foods, with additional carry/storage options.</p></div>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445881\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445881\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445881\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-2-00004-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-2-00004-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-2-00004.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The small size of the B10 makes it ideal for single portion meals or post-workout smoothies, with an assortment of optional accessories which expand upon the portability factor. The compact vessel is also great for preparing condiments like salad dressings, dips or even for quickly pulsing eggs for the fluffiest omelettes in manageable portions.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445883\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445883\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445883\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/BEAST-HEALTH-00014-SQUARE.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/beast-health/products/b10-health-blender\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Beast Health B10 Blender</a> is available for $138 in either Carbon Black, Pebble Grey or Cloud White, and includes a 1000mL blending vessel, drinking lid with carry cap, storage lid, blender base and B10 blade assembly. There&#8217;s also a <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/beast-health\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">selection of accessories</a> to expand /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Spanish creative agency Masquespacio, best <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/Masquespacio/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">known for their visually delightful spaces and branding</a>, returns with a new <a href=\"https://masquespacio.com/en/bun-burgers-bligny/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">project</a> marking their first one in Milan, Italy. Located next to Bocconi University at Viale Bligny, Bun is part of an Italian hamburger chain that was looking to appeal to a younger crowd while also representing the sophistication of a top notch burger restaurant. Instead of the typical vintage and industrial look of most hamburger chains they&#8217;ve seen, <a href=\"https://masquespacio.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Masquespacio</a> created a fresh approach to reflect Bun&#8217;s ethos.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445686\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445686\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445686\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/MASQUESPACIO-Bun-Hamburger-Chain-Milan-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/MASQUESPACIO-Bun-Hamburger-Chain-Milan-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/MASQUESPACIO-Bun-Hamburger-Chain-Milan-2-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/MASQUESPACIO-Bun-Hamburger-Chain-Milan-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/MASQUESPACIO-Bun-Hamburger-Chain-Milan-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Masquespacio&#8217;s design begins with an enticing avocado green and lavender color scheme that&#8217;s punctuated with wooden accents and gold details. Working with and expanding on the original elements of the space, including the bricks and arches, a cohesive plan formed throughout to welcome visitors into an innovative environment to enjoy their food.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445687\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445687\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large Launches Its First-Ever Sofa Designed by Takagi Homstvedt\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>In partnership with <a href=\"https://www.dims.world/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Dims.</a>, a direct-to-consumer contemporary furnishings brand, <a href=\"https://takagi-homstvedt.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Takagi Homstvedt</a> has designed the company’s first-ever sofa, the <a href=\"https://www.dims.world/products/alfa-sofa\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Alfa</a>. Inspired by the sleek curves of Italian cars in the 60s, the Alfa sofa is characterized by its rounded silhouette. The cushions are noticeably plush yet tidy, giving the sofa its structured look. Another distinguishing feature is the long legs that disappear into the sofa’s upswept backside, balancing the design’s substantial size with an element of lightness.</p>\n<p><a https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/dims-takaji-homestvedt-alfa-sofa-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The Alfa is offered in a 3-seater and a 2-seater option in six sustainably-produced Kvadrat textile colorways: Primer Green, Mélange Blue, Shell Pink, Toasted Ecru, Ikat Red and Off-White. The legs are available in Ash Wood and Black Powder-Coated Steel. Today, the Alfa sofa is available at <a href=\"https://www.dims.world/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">dims.world</a>.</p>\n<p><a 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"The ONDE Collection Blurs Form + Function","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445378","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/the-onde-collection-blurs-form-function/gandiablasco-onde-luca-nichetto-21/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-21-810x517.jpg\" alt=\"The ONDE Collection Blurs Form + Function\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>As time goes on it seems the line between indoor and outdoor furniture continues to blur, with the latest example being the <a href=\"https://www.gandiablasco.com/en/coleccion/onde/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">ONDE Collection</a>. Designed by <a href=\"https://www.gandiablasco.com/en/disenador/luca-nichetto/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Luca Nichetto</a> for <a href=\"https://www.gandiablasco.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">GANDIABLASCO</a>, this innovative group of 14 outdoor furniture pieces challenge the limits with a beautiful look that lies somewhere between Italian and Scandinavian. ONDE is as visually pleasing as it is functional, with modular capabilities that allow you to maximize on configuring spaces. But Nichetto&#8217;s design hallmark lies in the legs, which feature a cross design reminiscent of office furniture aesthetics. You&#8217;ll find this series just as at home in public spaces as in residential.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445725\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445725\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445725\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-Featured-Image-810x538.jpg\" alt=\"outdoor furniture on patio\" width=\"810\" height=\"538\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-Featured-Image-810x538.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-Featured-Image-800x531.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-Featured-Image-768x510.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-Featured-Image.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445712\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445712\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445712\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-2-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"outdoor chair\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-2-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-2-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-2-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-2-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<blockquote><p>Outdoor spaces are becoming more popular because the new generation of users are starting to make more life out of them and are taking the designs they usually use for indoor spaces to the outdoors. The key to ONDE is that it is able to create environments that can work in very different situations.</p></blockquote>\n<p><em>– Luca Nichetto, Designer</em></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445713\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445713\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445713\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-3-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"outdoor furniture\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-3-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-3-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-3-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-3-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/GANDIABLASCO-ONDE-Luca-Nichetto-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The complete ONDE Collection includes armchairs, two and three seat sofas, four different modules and a pouf. Made of welded thermo-lacquered aluminum and corrugated aluminum sheet, you have your choice of 15 colors from neutral to bold. ONDE even allows for the option of two-colored legs when you choose Copper. Included in the collection are also five models of low tables, with surfaces made of Dekton by Cosentino and available in a range of 11 colors.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445714\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445714\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445714\" Barber","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445763","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/clever-ep-143-industrial-designer-edward-barber/edward-barber-alisa-connan_bw_featured/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_featured-810x644.jpg\" alt=\"Clever Ep. 143:  Industrial Designer Edward Barber\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=\"attachment_445764\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"http://www.cleverpodcast.com/blog/ep-143-edward-barber\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><img loading=\"lazy\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_EB-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445764\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_EB-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_EB-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_EB-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_EB-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/edward-barber-Alisa-Connan_BW_EB.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Alisa Connan</p></div>\n<p>In <a href=\"http://www.cleverpodcast.com/blog/ep-143-edward-barber\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">this episode of Clever podcast</a>, Amy Devers talks to designer Edward Barber, who grew up in a small UK village running around with his brothers, making tree houses, bows and arrows, and drawing. As a teenager, he fell in love with sailing, fixing boats, and photography. He eventually landed in the architecture program at Royal College of Art where in the first week he met Jay Osgerby. The two became fast friends, collaborators and founding partners of Barber Osgerby. In the early years, with some “engineered luck” in the form of Giulio Cappellini, Edward and Jay were fast-tracked in the world of international furniture design. Since then, they’ve gone on to found Universal, an architecture and interior design studio, and Map, focused on tech and industrial design. Having designed everything from stacking chairs with a dynamic tilt aimed at improved learning in schools, to experiential sound installations&#8230; carving out his own path has worked out just fine!</p>\n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"188\" src=\"https://embed.acast.com/clever/cleverep.143-industrialdesigneredwardbarber\" scrolling=\"no\" frameborder=\"0\" 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"Work & Co’s New Office by Aspekt Office Feels Right at Home","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445916","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/work-cos-new-office-by-aspekt-office-feels-right-at-home/workco-aspekt-office-14/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-14-810x532.jpg\" alt=\"Work &#038; Co’s New Office by Aspekt Office Feels Right at Home\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://work.co/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Work &#38; Co</a> has offices in Brooklyn, Portland, Sao Paolo, Rio de Janeiro and Belgrade and each of them were designed with elements that considered their specific location. For the company’s new office in Copenhagen, it tapped on multidisciplinary design studio <a href=\"https://aspektoffice.com/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Aspekt Office</a> to create a workplace that’s homey, comfortable and quintessentially Danish.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445925\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445925\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445925\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-9-810x533.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-9-810x533.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-9-800x526.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-9-768x505.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-9.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445926\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445926\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445926\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-10-810x1218.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1218\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-10-810x1218.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-10-800x1203.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-10-768x1154.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-10-1022x1536.jpg 1022w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-10.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445918\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445918\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445918\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-2-810x511.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"511\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-2-810x511.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-2-800x504.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-2-768x484.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The new office is located in a century-old building originally designed by Danish architect Arthur Wittmaack in 1916. Aspekt Office pulls the building into modern times by giving it a Brutalist grid-modernism feel. The space is flooded with natural light, creating a warm and cozy atmosphere, and the choice of materials of oak wood, soothing neutrals and soft textiles help uphold that aesthetic. All fixed furnishings were designed by Aspekt Office, including a wall-to-wall bookcase with a built-in alcove in oak veneer, a soundproof phone booth, and the kitchen’s six-meters-long, custom-made table. The kitchen also houses the first ever <a href=\"https://www.reformcph.com/us/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Reform</a> x Aspekt Office kitchen, which is set to launch later this year.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445919\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445919\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445919\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-3-810x539.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"539\" https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-3-768x511.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445920\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445920\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/workco-aspekt-office-24.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The furniture was picked for their simple designs to contribute to the clean, minimalist look of the office. Being that the office is in Copenhagen, it was only logical that the team chose a mix of Scandinavian brands.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445938\" rel=\"attachment Home","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445817","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a recently completed the AR Residence <a href=\"http://dedraft.co.uk/projects/ar-residence/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">project</a> involving a renovation and extension added to a terraced Walthamstow house in London. The backyard offered enough space for a single-story, ground floor addition which also matched the depth of the neighbor&#8217;s own addition leaving enough room for the garden to breathe. The creative owners, an illustrator and librarian, opted for an extension that stands out amongst a sea of mundane structures. Their love of the color green led to <a href=\"http://dedraft.co.uk/home/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">DEDRAFT</a> selecting a matte dusty green to cover the custom folded aluminum panel system that wraps the new addition. Vertical fins pop out from the metal surfaces to add depth to the exterior facade while upping the character.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445820\" rel=\"attachment 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The added square footage allows for a new kitchen and dining room featuring exposed structural Douglas Fir ceiling joists. .jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn85@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-51-141_32a7cbf4668794fd.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/AR-Residence-DEDRAFT-London-24-810x1049.jpg":null,"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/AR-Residence-DEDRAFT-London-25-810x981.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn51@2020_6/2021/04/07/17-38-50-121_7e7182f819314ff7.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/AR-Residence-DEDRAFT-London-26-810x1034.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn41@2020_1/2021/04/07/17-38-50-593_7d025050a7a3375a.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/AR-Residence-DEDRAFT-London-27-810x1134.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn78@2020_4/2021/04/07/17-38-52-202_7216af413eff7a53.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/AR-Residence-DEDRAFT-London-28-original-810x1080.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn63@2020_2/2021/04/07/17-38-52-168_38d30ad612c37fc5.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/07ge-R3xtw0":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn11@2020_1/2021/04/07/17-38-49-495_6a168584b2d71434.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617817081505},{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"Lexus Design Award 2021 Selects 6 Innovative Finalists","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445562","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><em>The following post is brought to you by the <a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=designmilk%20&#38;utm_medium=article0406&#38;utm_campaign=designmilk_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Lexus Design Award</a>. Our partners are hand-picked by the Design Milk team because they represent the best in design.</em></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/lexus-design-award-2021-selects-6-innovative-finalists/lexus-design-award-trophy-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Trophy-Featured-Image-810x538.png\" alt=\"Lexus Design Award 2021 Selects 6 Innovative Finalists\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Next-generation talents have been competing for the <a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=designmilk%20&#38;utm_medium=article0406&#38;utm_campaign=designmilk_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Lexus Design Award</a> since its 2013 debut, taking on the challenge of creating Design for a Better Tomorrow. This year marks the ninth year of the international competition, with an impressive 2,079 entries submitted from 66 countries! A distinguished panel of jurors have narrowed down the pool to six finalists whose ideas embody the three principles of the Lexus Design Award – Anticipate, Innovate and Captivate. What’s on the line? A once-in-a lifetime experience to prototype their ideas with a project budget of ¥3,000,000 (approximately $25,000).</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445565\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445565\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445565\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-CY-BO-Kenji-Abe-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"packing material\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-CY-BO-Kenji-Abe-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-CY-BO-Kenji-Abe-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-CY-BO-Kenji-Abe-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-CY-BO-Kenji-Abe-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-CY-BO-Kenji-Abe.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em><strong>CY-BO by Kenji Abe (Japan)<br />\n</strong></em>CY-BO packing materials can be transformed into various shapes by combining different pieces. The material is formed out of a sponge-like material, and by overlapping it the interior becomes highly cushioned. The pieces can be rearranged any number of times, not only as packaging materials, but also pen cases, baskets, lamp shades, and more. CY-BO envelops fruits and dishes, and can even be used as a coaster thanks to its excellent water resistance. This product ultimately helps cut down on the discard of packing materials and can be reused as many times as possible.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445566\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445566\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445566\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445566\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Kenji-Abe-Headshot-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"Kenji Abe headshot\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Kenji-Abe-Headshot-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Kenji-Abe-Headshot-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Kenji-Abe-Headshot-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Kenji-Abe-Headshot-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Kenji-Abe-Headshot.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Kenji Abe</p></div>\n<p>In mid-January, the finalists attended a five day workshop where they were mentored by leading design experts Joe Doucet, Sabine Marcelis, Mariam Kamara and Sputniko!. The mentors’ love of guiding young talent partnered with a challenging curriculum gave way to fully engaged sessions for the finalists.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445568\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445568\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445568\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"handheld tech devices\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em><strong>Heartfelt by Gayle Lee and Jessica Vea (New Zealand &#38; Tonga, based in New Zealand)</strong></em><br />\nA live-streamed funeral was the starting point of Heartfelt, a device that enables virtual hugs. Providing an emotional connection when apart from your loved ones, such as during the pandemic, the product works in long-distance pairs. While one person cradles their device in their hands, the other device will warm to the same temperature at the same time. The temperature reflects the person holding it, and if not being held, will drop to room temperature (neutral). An LED is used to create a visual expression of both heartbeats – two differing LEDs pulsing at the same time, each half of the heart lit up in different colors to represent each user.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445567\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445567\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445567\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445567\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-Headshots-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"Gayle Lee and Jessica Vea headshots\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-Headshots-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-Headshots-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-Headshots-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-Headshots-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Heartfelt-Gayle-Lee-Jessica-Vea-Headshots.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Gayle Lee and Jessica Vea</p></div>\n<p>Once the workshop finished, Mariam Kamara said, &#8220;I was struck by the level of optimism and commitment the finalists have shown in their designs. In this new COVID-19 reshaped world, their visions and sensitivity is a gift to us all. Each one of them was incredibly passionate about the projects and demonstrated a strong motivation to delve deeper and do the necessary research to strengthen the final result. Though the mentoring was remote, a combination of powerful online tools and well-prepared finalists made for a fluid, productive and enjoyable process. I look forward to seeing where they take their designs in the coming months.&#8221;</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445570\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445570\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445570\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"interactive gloves\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-810x608.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em><strong>InTempo by Alina Holovatiuk (Ukraine)</strong></em><br />\nInTempo mitts may help distract the user from stressful situations through the use of rhythm and music. Rhythm therapy has the potential to replace medications, alcohol and therapy visits to improve the psychological state of a person. Fingerprint-shaped touch buttons on the palm side consist of five layers that form a durable touch panel. The outer and central layers are conductive, while two more insulating layers live on either side of the central one. When touched, the layers are compressed, forming a closed electric circuit. These influences are measured and interpreted using electronic controllers that convert the action into a signal for a controlled electronic device (player, smartphone, computer, etc). Touches on the four fingerprint fields are then registered and synchronized with the rhythm of the melody that is playing. When the rhythm coincides, the lower part of the mitt above the wrist will vibrate briefly as a reward.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445569\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445569\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445569\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445569\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-Headshot-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Alina Holovatiuk headshot\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-Headshot-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-Headshot-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-Headshot-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-InTempo-Alina-Holovatiuk-Headshot.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Alina Holovatiuk</p></div>\n<p>The finalists will continue to work with their mentors through the development of their prototypes as we grow closer to the Grand Prix selection. A judging panel of renowned design leaders awaits their finished projects: Paola Antonelli, Dong Gong, Greg Lynn and Simon Humphries will select Grand Prix Winner based on their final prototypes and presentations later this month.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445572\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445572\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445572\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"reactive fabric\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em><strong>KnitX by Irmandy Wicaksono (Indonesia, based in USA)</strong></em><br />\n3D knitting with computerized machines enable users to personalize their own textile patterns and structures through visual programming and a variety of yarns. KnitX is a computational and functional design principle for textile-based interactive surfaces. Functional yarns – such as resistive, conductive, thermochromic, photochromic and thermoplastic – are integrated to create responsive sensing (proximity, pressure, touch, and stretch) and actuation (color-changing and heating) capabilities. This approach allows for the rapid fabrication of seamless, responsive multi-dimensional textiles for applications from fashion to architecture. Demonstrations of possible work include: a musical fabric skin that allows users to interact and play discrete notes, harmonies, and soundscapes, a photochromic seamless knit textile that responds to UV and sunlight and a 3D responsive textile fabricated through thermoforming.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445571\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445571\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445571\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445571\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-Headshot-810x601.jpg\" alt=\"Irmandy Wicaksono headshot\" width=\"810\" height=\"601\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-Headshot-810x601.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-Headshot-800x594.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-Headshot-768x570.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-KnitX-Irmandy-Wicaksono-Headshot.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Irmandy Wicaksono</p></div>\n<p>Lexus Design Award 2021 judge Greg Lynn said, “In the middle of a changing climate and a global pandemic there was a predictable urgency to the problems being addressed by the designers. Across all the proposals we saw, there was also a humanity and intimate scale.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445574\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445574\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445574\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-810x539.jpg\" alt=\"desalination invention\" width=\"810\" height=\"539\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-810x539.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-768x511.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em><strong>Solar Desalination Skylight by Henry Glogau (New Zealand &#38; Austria, based in Denmark)</strong></em><br />\nChile currently has around 110,000 families living within 800 informal settlement communities. They live off the grid, devoid of services like water, electricity and sanitation. Windows are boarded up for security, privacy and protection from the environment and let in little natural light. An alternative to hacking the system could be the Solar Desalination Skylight. The prototype uses solar energy and seawater to create a product that emits naturally diffused light, produces drinking water and utilizes leftover salt brine for energy creation. Salt brine waste further used to create a source of energy when placed in storage tubes holding copper and zinc. These 12 salt batteries provided 9.53 volts, powering an LED light strip during the night and charged by a mini solar panel during the day. The desalinated water also adds a dappled effect to the lighting that changes moods throughout the day, creating a soft ambience for the living room space where family activities take place.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445573\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445573\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445573\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445573\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-Headshot-810x539.jpg\" alt=\"Henry Glogau headshot\" width=\"810\" height=\"539\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-Headshot-810x539.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-Headshot-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-Headshot-768x511.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-Headshot.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Henry Glogau</p></div>\n<p>Stay tuned as the Grand Prix Winner will be announced April 27th! To learn more about the Lexus Design Award, visit <a href=\"https://discoverlexus.com/experiences/lexus-design-award-2021?utm_source=designmilk%20&#38;utm_medium=article0406&#38;utm_campaign=designmilk_lda2021\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">LexusDesignAward.com</a>.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445576\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445576\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-445576\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-810x506.jpg\" alt=\"subway\" width=\"810\" height=\"506\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-810x506.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-800x500.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-768x480.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><em><strong>Terracotta Valley Wind by Intsui Design (China, based in Japan)</strong></em><br />\nIf you’ve ever ridden a subway in July, you know just how warm it can get on the platform. Heat from the trains and the people only manage to add pressure to any sort of air-conditioning that’s running in the station, leading to higher amounts of energy consumption. Terracotta Valley Wind could change it all, acting as a cooling wall made of spliced terracotta slabs with a water supply system (ideally using reclaimed water). The material has wonderful cooling properties and is cheap, while its porous nature allows water to move easily through the walls. By transmuting water to air it absorbs a relatively large amount of heat, effectively reducing the temperature of the environment.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445575\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445575\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445575\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445575\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-Headshots-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"Intsui Design headshot\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-Headshots-810x608.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-Headshots-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-Headshots-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-Headshots.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Intsui Design</p></div>\n<p>The water evaporates even faster with the wind of the passing trains, creating a cooling effect in the subway station. The whole system is pollution-free and doesn’t require any electricity.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/548QbgyTZAY\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" d-Solar-Desalination-Skylight-Henry-Glogau-Headshot-810x539.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn29@2020_6/2021/04/07/17-38-50-746_a2a619f3cc462852.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-810x506.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn51@2020_6/2021/04/07/17-38-52-346_2a75f3361fd859b6.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/Lexus-Design-Award-Solar-Terracotta-Valley-Wind-Intsui-Design-Headshots-810x608.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn94@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-51-293_e8beacd8b3155b37.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/548QbgyTZAY":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn20@2020_3/2021/04/07/17-38-49-583_b0a9d6dffc950423.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617817081502},{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"DMTV Milkshake: Francesca Bucci on Creating Hospitality at Sea","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=445759","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/dmtv-milkshake-francesca-bucci-on-creating-hospitality-at-sea/2-celebrity-flora_discovery-lounge/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/2-Celebrity-Flora_Discovery-Lounge-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"DMTV Milkshake: Francesca Bucci on Creating Hospitality at Sea\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>This week’s <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/DMTV-Milkshake/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">DMTV Milkshake</a> guest is Francesca Bucci, the Rome-born architect and founder of <a href=\"https://bgstudio.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">BG Studio International</a>. Bucci practices hospitality on a grand scale – like 100,000 square feet of interiors for the Celebrity Flora super-yacht, specially designed to explore the fragile ecosystem of the Galapagos Islands. “Even well before the pandemic, travelers were increasingly looking for different types of experiences – and to experience cruising in new ways, whether somewhere off the grid or to places that were protected or private,” she says. “This led to the development of vessels that were smaller and could access different places – vessels that were more sustainable, and with more outdoor spaces. Designing Celebrity Flora for Celebrity Cruises – a sustainable uber-yacht just for 100 guests with 50 suites, and truly purpose-built to navigate in the Galapagos Islands – was a groundbreaking experience for us and for the industry.”</p>\n<p><iframe title=\"YouTube video player\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/A_WqOmoDf64\" width=\"810\" height=\"455\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445797\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445797\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-445797\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-445797\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/1-Celebrity-Flora_Lounge-810x567.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"567\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/1-Celebrity-Flora_Lounge-810x567.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/1-Celebrity-Flora_Lounge-800x560.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/1-Celebrity-Flora_Lounge-768x538.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/04/1-Celebrity-Flora_Lounge.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Celebrity Flora® Lounge</p></div>\n<p>In this episode of Milkshake, Bucci also explores the many challenges of working in that environment, along with the responsibilities of designing for what is essentially a “captive audience,” Bucci says: “We’re always asking is, ‘What is the best experience that we can give to the guests and what can we offer them?’ We&#8217;re really focused on board experience – from culinary to spa, to recreation to fitness – and learning experiences, which are fundamental for the guests, as they become more and more sophisticated and really enjoy experiencing things that they don&#8217;t usually experience at home.” She also shares her larger philosophy on the tenets of hospitality – and how they might be applied to slightly inhospitable places, like drop-in medical clinics or the ever-humbler post office. “This is a place where most of us go often,” she says. “Wouldn&#8217;t it benefit from a facelift, to make the waiting and the sending experience a little bit less painful?”</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_445801\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445801\" travel.</em></p>\n<p><em><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/DMTV-Milkshake/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Milkshake</a>, DMTV (Design Milk TV)’s first regular series, shakes up the traditional interview format by asking designers, creatives, educators and industry professionals to select interview questions at random from their favorite bowl or vessel. passions.</em></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/2r92v08nYh8\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"Casey McCafferty Creates Unique Sculptural Furniture + Art","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=442570","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/casey-mccafferty-creates-unique-sculptural-furniture-art/casey-mccafferty-byzantium-small-table-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Casey-McCafferty-Byzantium-Small-Table-Featured-Image-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Casey McCafferty Creates Unique Sculptural Furniture + Art\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://www.casey-mccafferty.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Casey McCafferty&#8217;s</a> creations seem to belong in both a gallery and a getaway cabin. His work exhibits traditional techniques mixed with a unique style of experimentation, reflecting natural surroundings and the boundaries that exist between craftsmanship, <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/art\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">art</a> and technique.</p>\n<p>&#8220;All of my work starts from chunks of material and is hand-carved. I&#8217;m a firm believer in direct carving, I don&#8217;t like to make accurate sketches or diagrams for my sculptural practice. I usually think about stories I have read or the world around me and let it come out in wood,&#8221; McCafferty shared. &#8220;I rarely know what the finished form will look like till I am 75% through with the work. I like to have a range of functional and non-functional sculptures.&#8221;</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_442734\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=442734\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-442734\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"size-large wp-image-442734\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Casey-McCafferty-Three-Tiered-Table-1-810x539.jpg\" alt=\"sculptural table\" width=\"810\" height=\"539\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Casey-McCafferty-Three-Tiered-Table-1-810x539.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Casey-McCafferty-Three-Tiered-Table-1-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Casey-McCafferty-Three-Tiered-Table-1-768x511.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Casey-McCafferty-Three-Tiered-Table-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">3 Tiered Table</p></div>\n<p>After a lackluster career in banking, McCafferty didn&#8217;t want anyone else&#8217;s opinions controlling his woodworking. &#8220;Five years ago I decided if I was to be happy, I need to go into the shop every day like a child. I need freedom and I need to be able to express myself with the medium I choose,&#8221; he said. McCafferty&#8217;s now working full-time on his sculptural practice. &#8220;I think when someone is truly engaged in their work you see it. You can feel the soul in the work.&#8221;</p>\n<p>This is just a slice of his <a href=\"https://www.casey-mccafferty.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">portfolio</a>, I promise you&#8217;re going to want to click over and explore more!</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_442736\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a 01:38:01","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:01","title":"Shingle Stool Pulls Triple Duty in Flexible Working Environments","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=444999","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/shingle-stool-pulls-triple-duty-in-flexible-working-environments/shingle-stool-studio-jungmann-radetz-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2021/03/Shingle-Stool-Studio-Jungmann-Radetz-Featured-Image-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Shingle Stool Pulls Triple Duty in Flexible Working Environments\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>A rocking stool, a container and a partition wall when stacked. <a href=\"https://www.jonathanradetz.com/projects/shingle/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Shingle</a> stool really does a <em>lot.</em> Designed by <a href=\"http://laurajungmann.de/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Laura Jungmann</a> and <a href=\"https://www.jonathanradetz.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Jonathan Radetz</a>, and named for the appearance of the edge of its rounded rockers, this piece of <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furnishings\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">furniture</a> is ready to take on the flexible working environments of today and tomorrow. The stool can act as mobile seating as well as visual or acoustic shielding in open office plans. Once stacked, you&#8217;ll notice how Shingle&#8217;s rounded edge turns into a graphic element – similar to a shingled roof! Flip the stool upside down and it can easily be carried as a container, handle and all. Shingle stools are made of Solid Textile Boards by <a href=\"https://www.kvadrat.dk/en/really\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">REALLY</a>, a wood-like material made from scraps of fabric and used as a sustainable board material in furniture and architecture.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=445223\" rel=\"attachment
